Features:
- Short, wrinkled, and smooth fur
- Black nose and eyes
- Pink tongue
- Black, brown, and white fur pattern
KB:
- IF Short, wrinkled, and smooth fur AND Black nose and eyes AND Pink tongue THEN Pug
- IF Short, wrinkled, and smooth fur AND Black nose and eyes AND Black, brown, and white fur pattern THEN Saint Bernard
- IF Short, wrinkled, and smooth fur AND Black nose and eyes AND Pink tongue THEN Sphynx
- IF Short, wrinkled, and smooth fur AND Black nose and eyes AND Black, brown, and white fur pattern THEN Persian
Rule Check:
- The extracted features match the IF conditions of the Pug rule: Short, wrinkled, and smooth fur, Black nose and eyes, and Pink tongue.
- The extracted features do not match the IF conditions of the Saint Bernard, Sphynx, and Persian rules.
Classification:
<response>Pug</response>
